TUR_OPDA_level_up = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_OPDA_3
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_OPDA_3
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_OPDA_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_OPDA_2
			add_idea = TUR_OPDA_3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = TUR_OPDA_1
		}

			add_idea = TUR_OPDA_2
		}
	}
	if = {

			has_idea = TUR_OPDA
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_OPDA
			add_idea = TUR_OPDA_1
		}
	}
}

TUR_yildiz_teskilati_factions_variable_round_value = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power
					value = 0
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power
					value = 0
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power = 0 }
		}
	}
}

				add_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era_no_navy
			}
		}
		if = {

				add_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era_no_navy_2
			}
		}
		if = {

				add_idea = TUR_army_of_bygone_era_no_navy_7

TUR_legitimacy_level_up = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_terrible }
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_terrible
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_high }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_high
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal
		}
	}
}
TUR_legitimacy_level_down = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_high }
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_high
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_normal
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_medium
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_legitimacy_terrible }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_legitimacy_terrible
			add_idea = TUR_legitimacy_low
		}
	}
}

ottoman_minority_variable_check_konstantiniyye = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			347 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_southslav_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurd_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_region scope = TUR }
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_konstantiniyye = 1 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			347 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_konstantiniyye = 2 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			347 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_konstantiniyye = 3 }
		}
	}
	if = {

			347 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			set_variable = { ottoman_minority_variable_konstantiniyye = 4 }
		}
	}
	if = {

			}
		}
		every_country = {

		}
	}
	if = {

			}
		}
